'connected' : 'disconnected'); updateServiceSelect(); renderAllocationItems(); calculateTotalDays(); } function setPrintLanguage(lang) { printLanguage = lang; document.querySelectorAll('.print-lang-option').forEach(opt => { const radio = opt.querySelector('input'); const isActive = radio.value === lang; opt.classList.toggle('active', isActive); radio.checked = isActive; }); } function calculateTotalDays() { const years = parseInt(document.getElementById('durationYears').value) || 0; const months = parseInt(document.getElementById('durationMonths').value) || 0; const weeks = parseInt(document.getElementById('durationWeeks').value) || 0; // Conversion: 1 year = 12 months, 1 month = 4 weeks, 1 week = 5 days const totalDays = (years * 12 * 4 * 5) + (months * 4 * 5) + (weeks * 5); document.getElementById('totalDaysDisplay').textContent = totalDays; return totalDays; } function extractSheetId(url) { const match = url.match(/\/d\/([a-zA-Z0-9-_]+)/); return match ? match[1] : null; } async function connectToSheet() { const url = document.getElementById('sheetsUrl').value.trim(); if (!url) { alert(currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'الرجاء إدخال رابط جوجل شيت' : 'Please enter a Google Sheets URL'); return; } sheetId = extractSheetId(url); if (!sheetId) { alert(currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'رابط غير صالح' : 'Invalid Google Sheets URL'); return; } await syncWithSheet(); } async function syncWithSheet() { if (!sheetId) { alert(currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'الرجاء الاتصال بشيت أولاً' : 'Please connect to a sheet first'); return; } try { const csvUrl = `https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/${sheetId}/export?format=csv`; const response = await fetch(csvUrl); if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to fetch'); const csvText = await response.text(); Papa.parse(csvText, { header: true, skipEmptyLines: true, complete: function(results) { processSheetData(results.data); } }); } catch (error) { alert('Error: ' + error.message); updateConnectionStatus('error'); } } function processSheetData(data) { if (!data || data.length === 0) { alert(currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'لا توجد بيانات' : 'No data found'); return; } const firstRow = data[0]; const columns = Object.keys(firstRow); let nameColumn = columns.find(col => col.toLowerCase().includes('service') || col.toLowerCase().includes('name') || col.toLowerCase().includes('description') || col.toLowerCase().includes('خدمة') ) || columns[0]; let priceColumn = columns.find(col => col.toLowerCase().includes('price') || col.toLowerCase().includes('cost') || col.toLowerCase().includes('amount') || col.toLowerCase().includes('سعر') ) || columns[1] || columns[0]; servicesDatabase = data.map(row => ({ name: String(row[nameColumn] || '').trim(), price: parseFloat(row[priceColumn]) || 0 })).filter(s => s.name && s.price > 0); if (servicesDatabase.length === 0) { alert(currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'لا توجد خدمات صالحة' : 'No valid services found'); return; } updateServiceSelect(); // showServicesTable() - hidden by design, services only shown in dropdown lastSyncTime = new Date(); const timeStr = lastSyncTime.toLocaleTimeString(currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'ar-SA' : 'en-US'); document.getElementById('lastSync').textContent = (currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'آخر تحديث: ' : 'Last sync: ') + timeStr; updateConnectionStatus('connected'); // services table stays hidden - only dropdown is used } function updateConnectionStatus(status) { const statusEl = document.getElementById('connectionStatus'); const t = translations[currentLanguage]; statusEl.classList.remove('connected', 'error'); if (status === 'connected') { statusEl.classList.add('connected'); statusEl.innerHTML = `✅ ${t.connected}`; } else if (status === 'error') { statusEl.classList.add('error'); statusEl.innerHTML = `❌ Error`; } else { statusEl.innerHTML = `📡 ${t.notConnected}`; } } function showServicesTable() { const container = document.getElementById('servicesTableContainer'); const t = translations[currentLanguage]; let html = ''; html += ``; servicesDatabase.forEach(service => { html += ``; }); html += '
${t.service}${t.price} (SAR)
${service.name}${service.price.toLocaleString()}

} function addDatabaseService() { const select = document.getElementById('databaseServiceSelect'); if (select.value === '') { alert(translations[currentLanguage].selectService); return; } const service = servicesDatabase[select.value]; const price = parseFloat(document.getElementById('customServicePrice').value); if (!name || !price || price <= 0) { alert(translations[currentLanguage].enterServiceDetails); return; } addServiceToProject(name, price, 'custom'); document.getElementById('customServiceName').value = ''; document.getElementById('customServicePrice').value = ''; } function addServiceToProject(name, price, type) { selectedServices.push({ name, price, type, id: Date.now() }); const t = translations[currentLanguage]; if (selectedServices.length === 0) { list.innerHTML = `

${currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'لم تتم إضافة خدمات بعد' : 'No services added yet'}
`; totalBox.style.display = 'none'; return; } let html = ''; let total = 0; selectedServices.forEach((service, index) => { total += service.price; const icon = service.type === 'database' ? '📋' : '✏️'; const source = service.type === 'database' ? t.fromSheets : t.custom; html += `

${icon} ${service.name}

${source}

SAR ${service.price.toLocaleString()}
`; }); list.innerHTML = html; totalBox.style.display = 'flex'; totalAmount.textContent = `SAR ${total.toLocaleString()}`; } function removeService(index) { selectedServices.splice(index, 1); updateSelectedServicesList(); } function switchTab(tab) { document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active')); document.querySelectorAll('.tab-content').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active')); event.target.closest('.tab').classList.add('active'); document.getElementById(tab + '-tab').classList.add('active'); } function addAllocationItem() { const id = Date.now(); allocationItems.push({ id, name: '', percentage: 0 }); renderAllocationItems(); } function removeAllocationItem(id) { allocationItems = allocationItems.filter(item => item.id !== id); renderAllocationItems(); } function updateAllocationItem(id, field, value) { const item = allocationItems.find(i => i.id === id); if (item) item[field] = value; updateAllocationTotal(); } function renderAllocationItems() { const container = document.getElementById('allocationItems'); if (allocationItems.length === 0) { container.innerHTML = ''; updateAllocationTotal(); return; } let html = ''; allocationItems.forEach(item => { html += `
SAR 0
`; }); container.innerHTML = html; updateAllocationTotal(); } function updateAllocationTotal() { const total = allocationItems.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (parseFloat(item.percentage) || 0), 0); const t = translations[currentLanguage]; document.getElementById('allocationTotal').textContent = `${t.totalPercentage}: ${total}%`; document.getElementById('allocationTotal').style.color = total === 100 ? 'var(--aanaab-green)' : '#dc3545'; } function calculateAndGenerate() { const t = translations[currentLanguage]; const projectName = document.getElementById('projectName').value.trim(); const projectPeriod = calculateTotalDays(); const proposalDate = document.getElementById('proposalDate').value || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]; if (!projectName) { alert(t.enterProjectName); return; } if (projectPeriod === 0) { alert(t.enterProjectPeriod); return; } const allocationTotal = allocationItems.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (parseFloat(item.percentage) || 0), 0); if (allocationTotal !== 100 && allocationItems.length > 0) { alert(t.percentageError + ' (Current: ' + allocationTotal + '%)'); return; } const positions = [ { id: 'clevel', name: 'C-Level', rate: 9000 }, { id: 'director', name: currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'مدير تنفيذي' : 'Director', rate: 5000 }, { id: 'manager', name: currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'مدير' : 'Manager', rate: 4000 }, { id: 'associate', name: currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'محترف' : 'Associate', rate: 2000 }, { id: 'analyst', name: currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'محلل' : 'Analyst', rate: 1500 } ]; let teamCost = 0; let teamBreakdown = []; positions.forEach(pos => { const allocation = parseFloat(document.getElementById(`${pos.id}-allocation`).value) || 0; const count = parseInt(document.getElementById(`${pos.id}-count`).value) || 0; if (allocation > 0 && count > 0) { const effectiveDays = projectPeriod * (allocation / 100); const cost = effectiveDays * pos.rate * count; teamCost += cost; teamBreakdown.push({ position: pos.name, count, allocation, effectiveDays, dailyRate: pos.rate, cost }); } }); let servicesCost = selectedServices.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.price, 0); const totalCost = teamCost + servicesCost; document.getElementById('teamCostDisplay').textContent = `SAR ${teamCost.toLocaleString()}`; document.getElementById('servicesCostDisplay').textContent = `SAR ${servicesCost.toLocaleString()}`; document.getElementById('totalCostDisplay').textContent = `SAR ${totalCost.toLocaleString()}`; generateDeliverables(allocationItems, teamCost, servicesCost, totalCost); generateProposal(projectName, projectPeriod, proposalDate, teamBreakdown, selectedServices, teamCost, servicesCost, totalCost); document.getElementById('resultsSection').classList.add('active'); document.getElementById('resultsSection').scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' }); } function generateDeliverables(items, teamCost, servicesCost, totalCost) { const grid = document.getElementById('deliverablesGrid'); if (items.length === 0) { items = [{ name: currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'المخرج 1' : 'Deliverable 1', percentage: 100 }]; } let html = ''; items.forEach(item => { const percentage = item.percentage / 100; const teamAmount = teamCost * percentage; const servicesAmount = servicesCost * percentage; const totalAmount = totalCost * percentage; html += `

${currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'فريق' : 'Team'}: SAR ${teamAmount.toLocaleString()} | ${currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'خدمات' : 'Services'}: SAR ${servicesAmount.toLocaleString()}
SAR ${totalAmount.toLocaleString()}
${item.percentage}%
`; }); grid.innerHTML = html; } function generateProposal(projectName, period, date, teamBreakdown, services, teamCost, servicesCost, totalCost) { const t = translations[printLanguage]; const formattedDate = new Date(date).toLocaleDateString(printLanguage === 'ar' ? 'ar-SA' : 'en-US', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' }); const refNumber = 'AANAAB-' + new Date().getFullYear() + '-' + Math.floor(Math.random() * 1000).toString().padStart(3, '0'); const isArabic = printLanguage === 'ar'; // Calculate duration breakdown const years = Math.floor(period / (12 * 4 * 5)); const remainingAfterYears = period % (12 * 4 * 5); const months = Math.floor(remainingAfterYears / (4 * 5)); const remainingAfterMonths = remainingAfterYears % (4 * 5); const weeks = Math.floor(remainingAfterMonths / 5); const days = remainingAfterMonths % 5; let durationText = ''; if (years > 0) durationText += `${years} ${isArabic ? 'سنة' : 'year'}${years > 1 ? (isArabic ? '' : 's') : ''} `; if (months > 0) durationText += `${months} ${isArabic ? 'شهر' : 'month'}${months > 1 ? (isArabic ? '' : 's') : ''} `; if (weeks > 0) durationText += `${weeks} ${isArabic ? 'أسبوع' : 'week'}${weeks > 1 ? (isArabic ? '' : 's') : ''} `; if (days > 0 || durationText === '') durationText += `${days} ${isArabic ? 'يوم' : 'day'}${days > 1 ? (isArabic ? '' : 's') : ''}`; let teamRows = ''; teamBreakdown.forEach(member => { teamRows += `${member.position}${member.count}${member.allocation}%${member.effectiveDays.toFixed(1)} ${isArabic ? 'يوم' : 'days'}SAR ${member.dailyRate.toLocaleString()}SAR ${member.cost.toLocaleString()}`; }); let servicesRows = ''; services.forEach(service => { const icon = service.type === 'database' ? '📋' : '✏️'; const source = service.type === 'database' ? t.fromSheets : t.custom; servicesRows += `${icon} ${source}${service.name}SAR ${service.price.toLocaleString()}`; }); const proposalHTML = `
عناب
AANAAB CONSULTING
${t.proposalDate} ${formattedDate}
${t.proposalRef} ${refNumber}
${t.proposalTitle}
${t.proposalSubject}

${t.proposalIntro}

📋 ${t.projectInfo}

${t.projectName}: ${projectName}
${t.projectDuration}: ${durationText} (${period} ${isArabic ? 'يوم عمل' : 'working days'})
${t.numberDeliverables}: ${allocationItems.length || 1}

🎯 ${t.scopeOfWork}

${t.scopeText}

👥 ${t.teamAllocation}

${teamRows}
${t.position} ${t.count} ${t.allocation} ${t.effectiveDays} ${t.dailyRate} ${t.totalCost}
${t.subtotalTeam} SAR ${teamCost.toLocaleString()}

🛠️ ${t.services}

${servicesRows.length > 0 ? servicesRows : ``}
${t.type} ${t.service} ${t.price}
${t.noServices}
${t.subtotalServices} SAR ${servicesCost.toLocaleString()}

📦 ${t.deliverables}

${allocationItems.length > 0 ? allocationItems.map((item, idx) => `
${idx + 1}. ${item.name}
${item.percentage}% ${isArabic ? 'من إجمالي المشروع' : 'of total project'}
SAR ${((totalCost * item.percentage / 100) || 0).toLocaleString()}
`).join('') : `
${isArabic ? 'لم يتم تحديد مخرجات' : 'No deliverables specified'}
`}

💰 ${t.investmentSummary}

${t.teamCosts} SAR ${teamCost.toLocaleString()}
${t.servicesOther} SAR ${servicesCost.toLocaleString()}
${t.totalInvestment} SAR ${totalCost.toLocaleString()}

📋 ${t.termsConditions}

  • ${t.paymentTerms}
  • ${t.validFor}
  • ${t.additionalWork}
  • ${t.allRates}

${t.closingParagraph}

عناب
${t.contactInfo}
${t.sincerely}
${t.aanaabTeam}
${t.generatedBy}
`; document.getElementById('proposalPreview').innerHTML = proposalHTML; } // ── Collect current proposal data ───────────────────────────────────── function getProposalData() { const projectName = document.getElementById('projectName').value.trim(); const clientNameEl = document.getElementById('clientNameInput'); const clientName = clientNameEl ? clientNameEl.value.trim() : (currentLanguage === 'ar' ? 'اسم العميل' : 'Client Name'); const proposalNumEl = document.getElementById('proposalNumInput'); const proposalNum = proposalNumEl ? proposalNumEl.value.trim() : ('AANAAB-' + new Date().getFullYear() + '-001'); const proposalDate = document.getElementById('proposalDate').value || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]; // Build deliverables list from allocationItems + total cost const totalEl = document.getElementById('totalCostDisplay'); const totalCost = totalEl ? parseFloat(totalEl.textContent.replace(/[^0-9.]/g,'')) || 0 : 0; const deliverables = allocationItems.map(item => ({ name: item.name || (printLanguage === 'ar' ? 'مخرج' : 'Deliverable'), quantity: '1', unitPrice: String((totalCost * (item.percentage / 100)).toFixed(2)), unit: printLanguage === 'ar' ? 'مقطوعة' : 'Lump Sum', specs: item.percentage + '%' })); // If no allocation items, use total cost as single line if (deliverables.length === 0) { deliverables.push({ name: projectName || (printLanguage === 'ar' ? 'المشروع' : 'Project'), quantity: '1', unitPrice: String(totalCost.toFixed(2)), unit: printLanguage === 'ar' ? 'مقطوعة' : 'Lump Sum', specs: '' }); } return { projectName, clientName, proposalNum, proposalDate, deliverables, lang: printLanguage }; } // ── Print: A4 with template look ───────────────────────────────────── function printProposal() { const isArabic = printLanguage === 'ar'; const data = getProposalData(); const VAT = 0.15; const fmt = n => Number(n).toLocaleString('en-US', {minimumFractionDigits: 2}); let tableRows = ''; let totExcl = 0, totVAT = 0, totIncl = 0; if (isArabic) { // Arabic table: RTL, 9 cols, green header data.deliverables.forEach((d, i) => { const qty = parseFloat(d.quantity) || 1; const price = parseFloat(d.unitPrice) || 0; const excl = qty * price; const vat = excl * VAT; const incl = excl + vat; totExcl += excl; totVAT += vat; totIncl += incl; tableRows += ` ${fmt(incl)} ${fmt(vat)} ${fmt(excl)} ${fmt(price)} ${d.specs||''} ${fmt(qty)} ${d.unit||'مقطوعة'} ${d.name} ${i+1} `; }); tableRows += ` إجمالي المشروع بدون ضريبة (رقماً): ${fmt(totExcl)} إجمالي الضريبة (رقماً): ${fmt(totVAT)} إجمالي المشروع شامل الضرائب: ${fmt(totIncl)}`; } else { // English table: 7 cols, blue header data.deliverables.forEach((d, i) => { const qty = parseFloat(d.quantity) || 1; const price = parseFloat(d.unitPrice) || 0; const excl = qty * price; const vat = excl * VAT; const incl = excl + vat; totExcl += excl; totVAT += vat; totIncl += incl; tableRows += ` ${i+1} ${d.name} ${fmt(qty)} ${fmt(price)} ${fmt(excl)} ${fmt(vat)} ${fmt(incl)} `; }); tableRows += ` Total ${fmt(totExcl)} ${fmt(totVAT)} ${fmt(totIncl)} `; } const today = new Date(data.proposalDate).toLocaleDateString(isArabic ? 'ar-SA' : 'en-US'); const arContent = `
عرض مالي رقم: ${data.proposalNum}
